1087:          <xsl:sort select="@name"/>
1088:          <xsl:variable name="PER02" select="current-grouping-key()"/>
1089:          <xsl:for-each-group select="current-group()" group-by="(position() - 1) idiv 3">
1090:             <xsl:element name="S_PER">
1091:                <D_366>
1092:                   <xsl:choose>
1093:                      <xsl:when test="$contactType = 'BillTo'">AP</xsl:when>
1094:                      <xsl:when test="$contactType = 'ShipTo'">RE</xsl:when>
1095:                      <xsl:otherwise>CN</xsl:otherwise>
1096:                   </xsl:choose>
1097:                </D_366>
1098:                <D_93>
1099:                   <xsl:value-of select="$PER02"/>
1100:                </D_93>
1101:                <xsl:for-each select="current-group()">
1102:                   <xsl:choose>
1103:                      <xsl:when test="(position() mod 4) = 1">
1104:                         <xsl:element name="D_365">
1105:                            <xsl:value-of select="./@type"/>
1106:                         </xsl:element>
1107:                         <xsl:element name="D_364">

2674:    <xsl:template name="findDelimeter" match="node() | @*">
2675:       <xsl:param name="characters" as="xs:string*" select="'*', '~', '^', '|', '%', '!', ')', '(', '$', '#', ':', '&gt;', '&lt;'"/>
2676:       <xsl:variable name="nodes-to-inspect" as="node()*" select="//text() | //@*"/>
2677:       <xsl:call-template name="FormatDelimiters">
2678:          <xsl:with-param name="delimToUse" select="               string-join(for $delimTest in $characters               return                  $delimTest[not($nodes-to-inspect[contains(., $delimTest)])], ',')"/>
2679:       </xsl:call-template>
2680:    </xsl:template>
2681:    <xsl:template name="FormatDelimiters">
2682:       <xsl:param name="delimToUse"/>
2683:       <xsl:variable name="tokenizeDelim" select="tokenize($delimToUse, ',')"/>
2684:       <xsl:choose>
2685:          <xsl:when test="number(count($tokenizeDelim)) &gt; 3">
2686:             
2687:             
2688:             
2689:             <xsl:value-of select="$tokenizeDelim[3]"/>
2690:          </xsl:when>
2691:          <xsl:otherwise>
2692:             
2693:             
2694:             
2695:             <xsl:value-of select="''"/>
2696:          </xsl:otherwise>
2697:       </xsl:choose>
2698:    </xsl:template>
2699: </xsl:stylesheet>
